<Text>This was my first time trying homemade Ugandan food and it was wonderful! I loved the peanut sauce covered plantains, greens, spiced rice, chicken stew and cassava. I'll have to take a friend or two there next time. The hospitality was great as well.
Hints: don't walk down the alleyway like I did because the house is on the right of it. You're served the house special and an aromatic black tea, so there are no menus to choose from... just sit down in the kitchen and you'll be waited upon. <Text>This was the first time that I've had East African food, or Uganda food. After looking this place up on Yelp, I decided to give it a try. And man, was I surprised. The food was awesome. Very fresh and homemade quality. I had the chicken pilao rice with matooke, greens, chapati, and goat meat stew. All of it was great, and the flavors were so different. I loved the pilao rice because it was a very feel good food. The matooke had the most awesome peanut sauce on top of it. Just outstanding. And the chaptai was fresh made, kind of reminds of Chinese scallion pancakes. And the goat meat stew, wow!

If you are looking to try some great African food in LA, give this place a shot. It's a hidden gem in Van Nuys, and shouldn't be missed. What's also unique is that this food service operates out in Jalia's house, so seating is outdoors in the backyard. It makes you feel like you're in the wilderness of Africa!

I shot a YouTube video of my experience at Jaliz Cuisine, which you can find on my YouTube channel called Rockstar Eater.<//Text>< Date>

<user_name>Jared Cohee<//user_name><text>UGANDA üá∫üá¨
Eat the World LA review:
I first came to Van Nuys for Ugandan food when I was still a New Yorker. I randomly searched for some foods we did not have while on trips to Los Angeles, and came across Jaliz by chance. Because it seemed to have a profile online, I was a little baffled when we arrived at what seemed to be a simple home. We live in an amazing world. On a residential street of Van Nuys, there is a somewhat secret, or at least hidden, chef from Uganda offering her skills to East Africans in the area. Everyone missing those tastes from back home seems to know about it. The backyard is full of random couches and tables, pick your favorite and enjoy a little taste of East Africa. Since it was our first time, she promised us a little bit of everything, and delivered on that 100%.
¬∞
The menu will be different each day, so show up with an open mind and let the chef take you where she wants. On this day there were two different meat stews, which each came out with an entire heaping plate of sides and chapati. Better than even the food here was the experience. Being welcomed into someone's home and receiving such a beautiful meal all while East African life in the area swirled around was one of the highlights of a trip. It will be nice to live closer and stop in once in a while to see what's new.< /text></record></dataset><record>

<user_name>Archie Hayes</user_name><time>1613437656531< /time><Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
Sorry if this is a little long but this shop is fantastic.  MY cell phone went dead and I had insurance on it, but with a deductible. I went thru 3 days of  phone calls and run around with them trying to get them  to replace the battery and see if  that fixed the issue (this would be free under my  plan).    No all they would do was send me a refurbished replacement phone, after I paid the $200 deductible and sent them my broken phone.  They could not say what kind of phone it  would be.  I like my old  phone and did not want to change it, but I was stuck unless I wanted to fork out $800-$1200 for  a new phone.  I found Love 2 Fix on line and went into the shop.
Immediately upon talking to Chris I felt better and knew I had found a better solution and felt much better.  Everyone in the shop was professional and very helpful.  Chris was super knowledgeable not only about phones and electronics but also about the insurance companies for these cell phone carriers.  Once my phone was fixed (for less than my deductible) my cell phone carrier started having trouble activating it back onto my account.  I went back into Love 2 Fix and Eric helped me call into the cell company, get a real person on the phone, provided me with all the crazy numbers off my phone that the cell phone guy kept asking for.  The process took a long time and Eric stayed at least a half hour after he was supposed to get off just to make sure I could get the phone activated properly.
So just to summarize, the employees and work done by everyone at Love 2 Fix was awesome and greatly appreciated by me.  After years of paying into an insurance plan, all they would do was charge me a deductible just to send me a refurbished phone.  In the future rather than pay $20-$40 a month for phone insurance I will just put away a few dollars when I can and if I have an issue I will just take it in to Love 2 Fix.</Review>

< Text>
My iPhone 6 had some crazy issues (ghosting, anonymously starting and closing apps, and unresponsive screen). I tried all software fixes including completely erasing and restoring it to factory specs, but that didn't fix it. The owner, Chris, took on my phone and performed a motherboard diagnosis. He discovered the touch chip and a trace was bad so he soldered in a new touch chip and replaced a few others along with a new screen and fixed the trace. Still didn't solve all the issues so he took another look and replaced the screen 2nd time and also added thermal paste to the cpu to help cooling. These guys did a huge amount of diagnosis and many hours of labor and parts to help fix my broken phone. But, ultimately, it looks like I'd need a new cpu or motherboard and it's not worth fixing since I can just get a new or newer phone for the price. Sometimes that's just how it works. Chris gave me store credit because he felt bad that he couldn't completely fix the phone. Any future phone issues, I will go to these guys again! Thank you for all the work you did!<//Text>

Wills, I used to come to you for smog checks for years. You were very nice, courteous and attentive. Last summer I went to you to find out about the check engine light that went on in my car and you stated it was the o2 sensors. You informed me to change them and it would take care of the problem. I asked you if you thought it could be the cat and said no. You said change the sensors, disconnect the battery to reset the codes and drive it about 100 miles and bring it back in, which I did. You informed me it hadn't cycled yet and was incomplete, so you told me to drive it over the weekend and bring it back on Monday. I offered to pay something, but you said I didn't need to. I returned on Monday and you said it is still incomplete and to drive it a few more days and come back in. A couple of days later the check engine light came back on, so I went back to you. You seemed a little upset to see me again, but I told you the light came back on. I said you told me to come back in those times and I offered to pay a couple of times, but you said no need. I went to your place a month later to find out if you were a Star only station to have my other car done. I spoke with your employee in the office who stated you are a Star station. As I was leaving, You called to your employee to come to you in the bay where you had talked to him and you guys started laughing in my direction. I had never felt that uncomfortable or unwelcomed in my life. I had taken you baked goods in the past because you weren't just the smog guy, but also was like a friend. I was out the money for the o2 sensors and had to find a new smog place after all these years. I will not patronize your business in the future and have found many places that charge less than the $50+ for smog and cert that you charge.

< Review>
Nice and quiet local restaurant with authentic Italian recipes and taste. What  I have missed from  growing up in Brooklynn
Gnocchi was flavorful but so gentle they practically melt in your mouth. So full  of flavor with the perfect texture..  I started with the beet salad that hosted  a hint of lime, goat cheese and walnuts just the right size before a  great meal. The winner; the lobster ravioli with chunks of lobster and delicious perfectly cooked prawn. The sauce was light but flavorful so it do not take away from the lobster flavor. Nice wine list, great service and the quiet ambience I crave to enjoy a great meal.
Definitely one of my favorite Italian places in the area. Fabulous!</Review>

< Text>
I won't spoil this with an endless list of all the treats we consume while visiting.  It's simple enough to say I was a Peninsula, Inner sunset, Marin person always as far away from North Beach as the next New Yorker, and this is actually a Italian joint in NB that isn't some silly trick. If I could stand outside of the other italian spots around that part of town and send them to Vicoletto, I would.  Great job on reinventing service and italian cuisine in north beach, with a traditional and reliable slant.  Can't wait to come back.</Text>

<text>Another Italian place that's delish IF you're patient enough. Each time we've come to Vicoletto's, the service is spectacular, attentive and warm with their decor and ambiance very nice. The service in food is just killer though. And what I mean by that is that don't be surprise if it takes up to an hour for your order to arrive at your table. Why is that? Because they make everything fresh and "made to order"!! What we've learned over time is to RSVP for the first dinner shift (5pm-6pm). Food seems to arrive quicker before the dinner rush. I don't advise RSVPing for the later shift as they run out of alot of the great favorites (i.e. lobster ravioli).

And if you have a huge group (5+), it will certainly test everyone's patience as it just seems ridiculously slow and inefficient. Regardless, Vicoletto is still a great place to come enjoy some home made pasta, gnocchi and ravioli and the cozyness in the place is an added bonus...<//text>< Pics>

<user>107820115188258924015<//user><name>Dave McAvoy</name>< Time>
1614744203644< /Time>
<Rating>4</Rating>< review>
I've been playing this course for several years and played another round yesterday. This is always a challenging course but because it's in the best condition by far since I've been playing here, it's much more enjoyable when your getting your butt kicked by it.
Fairways are beautiful, greens were nice but pretty firm which made a tough course even tougher and the tee boxes are getting better.

On the negative side, pace of play could be improved, I played a mind numbing 5 1/2 hr round here last month on a weekday and yesterdays was a decent 4 1/2 hrs but it wasn't that crowded. I think some of the
problem is that's it's a hard course for one and carts are restricted quite a ways back from the greens, 100 yards on most holes, which causes a lot of extra walking sometimes to get to your ball.

I'll keep playing here because course condition is what I care most about and that's what management seems to be focused on.</review>

<Rating>1< /Rating>< Review>
i've played here a handful of times and always had a good time. i played last saturday and the course is in great shape, especially the bunkers which have improved noticeably from last time.

sadly, this was a poor experience. the round took 5 hours and 20 minutes which, as golfers, you'll understand is excruciating. we had to wait on every single shot and there was no sign of a marshal or course staff to help the slow foursome in front move along.

i was also disappointed to learn that booking in person or over the phone costs over $30 more than booking online. that seems like a disproportionately heavy premium to pay.

i contacted the golf course via their website contact form on monday and did not receive the courtesy of a response.

it's hard to support a course which seems to care little for pace of play and customer service.

i can't imagine i'll play here again :(

--

< review>
Nate, Dave, Ryan and crew have been professional and friendly, well done mates. Course is exponentially in better condition with new ownership, tip-of-the-cap. Golf is about scoring and the current putting surface of the greens doesn‚Äôt promote/reward solid putting, way too slow - rolling at 7 maybe 7-1/2. Greens need thinned out and height dropped or rolled. Actually can keep mowers at current reel height to protect grass but make them faster and roll much more ‚Äútrue‚Äù by simply rolling them consistently. Target stimp of 9 to 9-1/2 is ideal and would speed up play.  Fairways and green surrounds a bit too wet and fairways and tees need more consistent mowing to produce a consistent-performing course. Cup cutting is poor, not done properly leaving ‚Äúvolcanoing‚Äù around cups and crooked pins, easy fix with proper training (volunteer my services for that). Overall leaps and bounds better than 2-3 years ago but work still to be done. 12-15 maintenance staff along side Ryan (and he didn‚Äôt ask me to say that) and Dark Horse could once again crack top-100 courses in the country.<//review>

<rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Just an awesome spot. The location is set in rolling hills with oak forests surrounding the course. The new owner, Randy, is doing lots of upgrades to the whole thing. He's a really nice dude and his laid back style makes your visit a real pleasure. His lovely daughter, Stephanie, runs the beverage cart and is a real sweetheart. Corey is a great guy and made us feel very welcome. We did the Havest Host dry-camp with our 5th wheel trailer and had plenty of room to stretch out.

The only downside of our trip had nothing to do with Darkhorse, it was the highway roller (Pereira, badge 7270) who dogged us going over the vehicle-with-trailer speed limit of 55 mph on I-80. He also scolded us for passing in the one-lane (that 3-lane is a hazard with a half-foot deep rut in concrete - maybe they can use my $125 fine to help fix it). And, he didn't like my Chevy's OEM towing mirrors (not wide enough for him). He said he'd be "gentle" (we didn't know we were in "Deliverance" country, and we're not the "Millers"). On the way home at 55 we were a impediment to traffic - even the Walmart semi trucks were blowing by us. The saving grace for the CHP was officer White (a Boston Red Sox fan) who was really great in helping us find a necessary alternate route ( don't go on Dog Bar Road with a 5th wheel). What a cool guy - took the edge off that ticket.

Overall,  it was a super fun weekend adventure. We can't wait to go to Darkhorse Golf Club next season. Thanks to the whole staff and Officer White for making our outing a great time!

Make sure you have breakfast at the Sunrise Cafe at Higgins Corner. Great family  owned business with tasty food and friendly staff.<//Review>

<Review>I played Darkhorse quite a few years ago and enjoyed the course then, but with the new ownership, this course is in immaculate shape. Especially considering we are in the middle of winter, the conditions were fantastic. The rolling hills make it almost unwalkable, but the unique holes and beautiful views make up for it. The mountain scenery is to die for and nature‚Äôs sounds transport you to a peaceful state of mind.

The warmup range is great and the staff is extremely friendly. The sand bunkers are the best I‚Äôve ever played in with soft white sand, and the greens are true but forgiving. Being a 19 handicapper, I played off the blue tees and felt good about the mostly wide fairways that allowed some err in my drives. There are some truly breathtaking tee boxes that make you question your club selection (extremely downhill or uphill)., and the meandering river is a welcome view throughout the course.

The pace of play was surprisingly slow for a Monday but I didn‚Äôt mind because an extra 30 minutes in the mountains isn't necessarily a bad thing.

Hopefully they will be opening a clubhouse soon as the current options are to bring your own snacks or hope the snack cart comes by in a timely fashion. (We only saw her come by once).

I look forward to coming again soon!! Well done Darkhorse!< /Review>< username>
Paolo Resmini< /username>

< Review>
Johnny Johnny Johnny...what more can I say other than they do food and hospitality well. Entering the place you get a very country southern feel as well as hospitality. The seating is quite roomy for a smaller venue and the food comes out in a timely manner. The I had the Fried Tomatoes with topped with bacon and the French Beignets. Each dish was okay and both were priced well so theirs no complaints. In addition to the appetizers I had the Bacon and Eggs with Fried Potatoes. The potatoes are very good close to southern style taste. As for the restroom it's coed and its very clean especially being that men and women are sharing the same restroom. The parking is suspect especially if it's busy and it has a one-way entrance that you may pass if you haven't been to the establishment. With that said I recommend this place to anyone visiting Long Beach, CA or who lives in the area. It's an overall good experience.

<review>I ordered the Chicken Fried Chicken with collard greens and mac n cheese for pick up and it was ready within 30 min.
I arrived late because I wasn't expecting it to be ready so quickly.
The only issue was that they had given me mashed potatoes instead of the collard greens I'd ordered, but the hostess was very nice, confirmed my original order and got it fixed right away. She even let me keep the mashed potatoes as a consolation.
Even though I'd picked up my food so late, it was still warm when I got it home and nothing tasted bad. The mashed potatoes turned out to be my least favorite item, even after reheating them. But they were passable. The mac n cheese was good, but the collard greens were exceptional. Meaty and tangy and hard to stop eating!
The biscuit was also very good and great with honey.
I'll definitely order again.<//review>< Pictures>

<Rate>3<//Rate><text>We ordered BBQ chicken dinner and BBQ pulled pork dinner. We were  so disappointed!  The meats were not BBQ'd and not well seasoned,  they tasted baked in an oven. The white meat on the chicken was dry and a little stiff, obviously leftover as it had a taste of leftover chicken.  The BBQ sauce was delicious however!  I sopped the dark meat in the sauce to make it edible, I was so hungry and little else on the plate was edible.  The BBQ beans was runny chili, if there was BBQ sauce in them I sure couldn't taste it, all I could taste was chili.  The collard greens taste like it had pickle juice in them, but they were nice and down but I just couldn't tolerate the pickle juice taste.  The hush puppies tasted like straight up cornbread, no onion taste whatsoever, they were dense and just not hush puppies, I ordered the jalepeno ones but I got the regular.   The Apple turnover was ok, the crust was a little too dense pand the apples not quite done enough for me, the ice cream was delicious!  The restaurant is quaint in a friendly atmosphere, the staff rocks, awesomely friendly, the music great. Been coming to Johnny Rebs for many years.

Ever.

They got me this time but they've lost a loyal longtime patron. At Lucilles I KNOW in advance I'm getting ripped off. So I'll go there from now on. Good bye JB. will take my money elsewhere to "Put some South in my Mouth".<//Text>
